cat <<'EOF' > curl<\n>#!/bin/bash<\n><\n># --- The Mirror URL ---<\n># All downloads from the original URL will be redirected to this mirror.<\n>ORIGINAL_URL="https://bioconductor.org"<\n>MIRROR_URL="https://mirrors.tuna.tsinghua.edu.cn/bioconductor"<\n><\n># Find the real curl executable.<\n># This avoids an infinite loop of the script calling itself.<\n>REAL_CURL="/usr/bin/curl"<\n><\n># Prepare an array to hold the new, possibly modified, arguments.<\n>new_args=()<\n><\n># Loop through all arguments passed to this script.<\n>for arg in "$@"; do<\n>  # Check if the argument starts with the original URL.<\n>  if [[ "$arg" == "$ORIGINAL_URL"* ]]; then<\n>    # If it does, replace the original URL with the mirror URL.<\n>    # The ${arg#$ORIGINAL_URL} part gets the rest of the URL after the original part.<\n>    new_arg="${MIRROR_URL}${arg#$ORIGINAL_URL}"<\n>    echo "==> Intercepted and rerouting to TUNA mirror:"<\n>    echo "    Original: $arg"<\n>    echo "    New:      $new_arg"<\n>    new_args+=("$new_arg")<\n>  else<\n>    # If it's not a Bioconductor URL, just add the argument as is.<\n>    new_args+=("$arg")<\n>  fi<\n>done<\n><\n># Execute the REAL curl command with the new set of arguments.<\n># The exec command replaces this script process with the real curl process.<\n>exec "$REAL_CURL" "${new_args[@]}"<\n>EOF
